<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

		

        function cityIsSelected(selectElement)
        {
            var cityAttr = $(selectElement.options[selectElement.selectedIndex]).attr('data-city');
            if (typeof cityAttr === 'undefined' || cityAttr === false)
            {
                return false;
            }
            return true;
        }


       function validateAvaSearch(selectDepartureDayId, selectDepartureMonthId, selectReturnDayId, selectReturnMonthId, selectDepartureCityId, selectArrivalCityId, tripTypeName)
        {
            var objSelectDepartureCity = document.getElementById(selectDepartureCityId);
            var objSelectArrivalCity = document.getElementById(selectArrivalCityId);
            
            if (objSelectDepartureCity.options[objSelectDepartureCity.selectedIndex].value == "" || objSelectDepartureCity.options[objSelectDepartureCity.selectedIndex].value == " ")
	        {
		        alert('Vælg afrejsepunkt');
		        return false;
	        }
            else if (!cityIsSelected(objSelectArrivalCity) || objSelectArrivalCity.options[objSelectArrivalCity.selectedIndex].value == "selectDestination" || objSelectArrivalCity.options[objSelectArrivalCity.selectedIndex].value == "" || objSelectArrivalCity.options[objSelectArrivalCity.selectedIndex].value == " ")
	        {
		        alert('Vælg destination');
		        return false;
	        }
	        else
	        {
		        return validateDates(selectDepartureDayId, selectDepartureMonthId, selectReturnDayId, selectReturnMonthId, tripTypeName, false);
	        }
        }

        function validateDates(selectDepartureDayId, selectDepartureMonthId, selectReturnDayId, selectReturnMonthId, tripTypeName, hideWarning)
        {
            var objSelectDepartureDay = document.getElementById(selectDepartureDayId);
            var objSelectDepartureMonth = document.getElementById(selectDepartureMonthId);
            var objSelectReturnDay = document.getElementById(selectReturnDayId);
            var objSelectReturnMonth = document.getElementById(selectReturnMonthId);
	        var errMesg = "";
            
            var departureDate = extractDate(objSelectDepartureDay, objSelectDepartureMonth);
            if (!isValidDate(departureDate))
                errMesg = errMesg + 'Afgangsdatoen er ikke gyldig\n';
            
	        if ($('input:radio[name=' + tripTypeName + ']:checked').val() == '2') {
                var returnDate = extractDate(objSelectReturnDay, objSelectReturnMonth);
                if (!isValidDate(returnDate))
                    errMesg = errMesg + 'Returdatoen er ikke gyldig\n';
                
		        if(returnDate < departureDate)
			        errMesg = errMesg + 'Udgående flyvning kan ikke ligge senere end returflyvning!\n';
	        }

	        var today = new Date();
	        if (new Date(departureDate.getFullYear(), departureDate.getMonth(), departureDate.getDate(), 23, 59, 59, 999) < today)
		        errMesg = errMesg + 'Afgangsdatoen er ikke gyldig\n';

	        if (errMesg.length > 0) {
		        if (!hideWarning)
			        alert(errMesg);
		        return false;
	        }
	        else 
		        return true;
        }

        function getAvaSearch   (selectDepartureDayId, selectDepartureMonthId, selectReturnDayId, selectReturnMonthId, selectDepartureCityId, selectArrivalCityId, tripTypeName, selectAdultsId, selectChildrenId, selectInfantsId)
        {

	        if (validateAvaSearch(selectDepartureDayId, selectDepartureMonthId, selectReturnDayId, selectReturnMonthId, selectDepartureCityId, selectArrivalCityId, tripTypeName))
	        {
                var objSelectDepartureCity = document.getElementById(selectDepartureCityId);
                var objSelectArrivalCity = document.getElementById(selectArrivalCityId);
                var objSelectDepartureDay = document.getElementById(selectDepartureDayId);
                var objSelectDepartureMonth = document.getElementById(selectDepartureMonthId);
                var objSelectReturnDay = document.getElementById(selectReturnDayId);
                var objSelectReturnMonth = document.getElementById(selectReturnMonthId);
                var objSelectAdults = document.getElementById(selectAdultsId);
                var objSelectChildren = document.getElementById(selectChildrenId);
                var objSelectInfants = document.getElementById(selectInfantsId);                
                var valTripType = $('input:radio[name=' + tripTypeName + ']:checked').val();
                var objSelectProcessMode = '';
                
                var query = '?D_City=' + objSelectDepartureCity.value + 
                            '&A_City=' + objSelectArrivalCity.value + 
                            '&TripType=' + valTripType + 
                            '&D_Day=' + objSelectDepartureDay.value + 
                            '&D_Month=' + objSelectDepartureMonth.value + 
                            '&R_Day=' + objSelectReturnDay.value + 
                            '&R_Month=' + objSelectReturnMonth.value + 
                            '&AdultCount=' + objSelectAdults.value + 
                            '&ChildCount=' + objSelectChildren.value + 
                            '&InfantCount='+ objSelectInfants.value;

                if(objSelectAdults.value == 'x')
                {
                    window.location.href = '/ssl/dk/processpages/grouptravel/grouptravelavaday/' + query;
                }
                else{
                    window.location.href = '/dk/fly/valg-flyvning/' + query;
                }
	        }
        }
		
		

        function cityIsSelected(selectElement)
        {
            var cityAttr = $(selectElement.options[selectElement.selectedIndex]).attr('data-city');
            if (typeof cityAttr === 'undefined' || cityAttr === false)
            {
                return false;
            }
            return true;
        }

        function farecalValidateDate(selectDepartureMonthId, selectReturnMonthId, hideWarning)
		{
            var objSelectDepartureMonth = document.getElementById(selectDepartureMonthId);
            var objSelectReturnMonth = document.getElementById(selectReturnMonthId);
			var errMesg = "";
                
            var returnMonth = objSelectReturnMonth.options[objSelectReturnMonth.selectedIndex].value;
            var departureMonth = objSelectDepartureMonth.options[objSelectDepartureMonth.selectedIndex].value;
            if (returnMonth != '' && (parseInt(returnMonth, 10) < parseInt(departureMonth,10))) {
                errMesg = errMesg + 'Udgående flyvning kan ikke ligge senere end returflyvning!\n';
			}
			if (errMesg.length > 0) {
				if (!hideWarning)
					alert(errMesg);
				return false;
			}
			else 
				return true;
		}
        
        function farecalValidate(selectDepartureMonthId, selectReturnMonthId, selectDepartureCityId, selectArrivalCityId)
		{
            var objSelectDepartureCity = document.getElementById(selectDepartureCityId);
            var objSelectArrivalCity = document.getElementById(selectArrivalCityId);
            var objSelectDepartureMonth = document.getElementById(selectDepartureMonthId);
            var objSelectReturnMonth = document.getElementById(selectReturnMonthId);  
            if (objSelectDepartureCity.options[objSelectDepartureCity.selectedIndex].value == "" || objSelectDepartureCity.options[objSelectDepartureCity.selectedIndex].value == " ")
			{
				alert('Vælg afrejsepunkt');
				return false;
			}
            else if (!cityIsSelected(objSelectArrivalCity) || objSelectArrivalCity.options[objSelectArrivalCity.selectedIndex].value == "" || objSelectArrivalCity.options[objSelectArrivalCity.selectedIndex].value == " ")
			{
				alert('Vælg destination');
				return false;
			}
			else
			{
				return farecalValidateDate(selectDepartureMonthId, selectReturnMonthId, false);
			}
		}

        function getFareCalendar(selectDepartureMonthId, selectReturnMonthId, selectDepartureCityId, selectArrivalCityId, selectAdultsId, selectChildrenId, selectInfantsId, tripType, selectedDepartureDay, selectedReturnDay)
		{
            var objSelectDepartureCity = document.getElementById(selectDepartureCityId);
            var objSelectArrivalCity = document.getElementById(selectArrivalCityId);
            var objSelectDepartureMonth = document.getElementById(selectDepartureMonthId);
            var objSelectReturnMonth = document.getElementById(selectReturnMonthId);                
            var objSelectAdults = document.getElementById(selectAdultsId);
            var objSelectChildren = document.getElementById(selectChildrenId);
            var objSelectInfants = document.getElementById(selectInfantsId); 
            var numAdults = 1;
            var numChildren = 0;
            var numInfants = 0;            

			if (farecalValidate(selectDepartureMonthId, selectReturnMonthId, selectDepartureCityId, selectArrivalCityId))
            {
                var valDCity = objSelectDepartureCity.value;
                var valACity = objSelectArrivalCity.value;
                var valDMonth = objSelectDepartureMonth.value;
                var valRMonth = objSelectReturnMonth.value;

                var valTripType;
                if(typeof(tripType)=='undefined' || tripType == null)
                {
			        if (objSelectReturnMonth.selectedIndex != 0) {
                       valTripType = 2; 
                    }
                    else {
                        valTripType = 1;
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    valTripType = tripType;
                }

                if (objSelectAdults != null && '' + objSelectAdults != 'undefined'){
                    numAdults = objSelectAdults.value;
                    numChildren = objSelectChildren.value;
                    numInfants = objSelectInfants.value;
                }
                
                var query = '?D_City=' + valDCity+ '&A_City=' + valACity + '&TripType=' + valTripType + '&D_Month=' + valDMonth + '&R_Month=' + valRMonth + '&AdultCount=' + numAdults + '&ChildCount=' + numChildren + '&InfantCount=' + numInfants;
                if(objSelectAdults != null && '' + objSelectAdults != 'undefined' && objSelectAdults.value == 'x')
                {
                    if(typeof(selectedDepartureDay)!='undefined' && selectedDepartureDay != null)
                    {
                        query += '&D_Day=' + selectedDepartureDay.value;
                    }
                    if(typeof(selectedReturnDay)!='undefined' && selectedReturnDay != null)
                    {
                        query += '&R_Day=' + selectedReturnDay.value;
                    }
                    window.location.href = '/ssl/dk/processpages/grouptravel/grouptravelavaday/' + query;
                }
                else{
                    if(typeof(selectedDepartureDay)!='undefined' && selectedDepartureDay != null)
                    {
                        query += '&D_Day=1&D_SelectedDay=' + selectedDepartureDay.value;
                    }
                    if(typeof(selectedReturnDay)!='undefined' && selectedReturnDay != null)
                    {
                        query += '&R_Day=1&R_SelectedDay=' + selectedReturnDay.value;
                    }
                    window.location.href = '/dk/fly/lavpris/' + query;
                }        
            }
		}

        //]]>
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

var countryPrefix = 'Country_';
function formatCountriesSelect2(city) {
    if (city.id.indexOf(countryPrefix) != -1) return "<div class='countryItem'>" + city.text + "</div>";
    else return city.text;
}
function formatCountries(selectElementId) {
    var selectElement = $(document.getElementById(selectElementId));
    if (selectElement) {
        var countryItems = selectElement.find("option[value*='" + countryPrefix + "']");
        if (countryItems && countryItems.length > 0) {
            $.each(countryItems, function(k, v) {
                $(this).addClass('countryItem');
                $(this).attr("disabled", "disabled");
            });
        }
    }
}
function select2CountryMatcher(searchTerm, displayName)
{
    if (searchTerm == '') return true;
    if (displayName.indexOf('-') == 0 || displayName.indexOf(' -') == 0) return false;
    var result =  displayName.toUpperCase().indexOf(searchTerm.toUpperCase()) >= 0;
    return result;
}
$(document).ready(function() {
    var select2Enabled = true; 
    var ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_selectedArrivalCity = '';

    $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureCity").change(function() {
        setIATAOptions($('#ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnArrivalCity'), listDestinations, $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureCity")[0].value, ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_selectedArrivalCity, select2Enabled);
    });

    setDeparture(document.getElementById("ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureCity"), 'CPH');
    setIATAOptions($('#ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnArrivalCity'), listDestinations, $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureCity")[0].value, '', select2Enabled);
    setArrival(document.getElementById("ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnArrivalCity"), '');
    $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnArrivalCity").change(function() {
        ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_selectedArrivalCity = $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnArrivalCity").val();
    });

    function DoSearchctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox() {

    function DoTrackingctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox() {
        if (getSearchTypectl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox('ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox') == 'FareCalendar') {
            _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'SearchBox - Front Page', 'AvaDayWithFareCalendarOption', 'FareCalendar']);
        } else {
            _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'SearchBox - Front Page', 'AvaDayWithFareCalendarOption', 'Avaday']);
        }
    }
    function getTripTypectl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox(clientId)
    {
        var tripType = $('input:radio[name=' + clientId + '_TripType]:checked').val();
        if(tripType == '2') {
            return '2';
        }else {
            return '1';
        }
    }
    function getSearchTypectl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl00_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox(clientId) {
        var searchType = $('input:radio[name=' + clientId + 'SearchType]:checked').val();
        if(searchType == 'FareCalendar') {
            return 'FareCalendar';
        }else {
            return 'Avaday';
        }
    }

<script type="text/javascript">
    function btnSendClick(){
        var urlField = document.getElementById('ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl01_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcNewsletterSignupUnit_hiddenPostUrl');
        var url = urlField.value;
        
        var emailaddressField = document.getElementById('ctl00_MainContentRegion_LeftColumnRegion_ctl01_ctl00_ctl01_ctl00_ipcNewsletterSignupUnit_txtEmailAddress');
        var emailaddress = emailaddressField.value;
        
        var tooltip = emailaddressField.title;
        
        if(url.length > 0 && emailaddress.length > 0){
            if(emailaddress != tooltip){
                url = url + "?email=" + emailaddress;
                document.location.href = url;
            }
        }
    }
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

var countryPrefix = 'Country_';
function formatCountriesSelect2(city) {
    if (city.id.indexOf(countryPrefix) != -1) return "<div class='countryItem'>" + city.text + "</div>";
    else return city.text;
}
function formatCountries(selectElementId) {
    var selectElement = $(document.getElementById(selectElementId));
    if (selectElement) {
        var countryItems = selectElement.find("option[value*='" + countryPrefix + "']");
        if (countryItems && countryItems.length > 0) {
            $.each(countryItems, function(k, v) {
                $(this).addClass('countryItem');
                $(this).attr("disabled", "disabled");
            });
        }
    }
}
function select2CountryMatcher(searchTerm, displayName)
{
    if (searchTerm == '') return true;
    if (displayName.indexOf('-') == 0 || displayName.indexOf(' -') == 0) return false;
    var result =  displayName.toUpperCase().indexOf(searchTerm.toUpperCase()) >= 0;
    return result;
}
$(document).ready(function() {
    var select2Enabled = true; 
    var ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_selectedArrivalCity = '';

    $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureCity").change(function() {
        setIATAOptions($('#ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnArrivalCity'), listDestinations, $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureCity")[0].value, ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_selectedArrivalCity, select2Enabled);
    });

    setDeparture(document.getElementById("ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureCity"), 'CPH');
    setIATAOptions($('#ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnArrivalCity'), listDestinations, $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureCity")[0].value, '', select2Enabled);
    setArrival(document.getElementById("ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnArrivalCity"), '');
    $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnArrivalCity").change(function() {
        ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_selectedArrivalCity = $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnArrivalCity").val();
    });
    $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureDay, #ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureMonth").change(function() {
        checkDateDisplay('ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureDay', 'ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureMonth', 'ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnReturnDay', 'ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnReturnMonth', 'ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_hiddenDepartureDate', 'ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_hiddenReturnDate', 'FareCalendar');
    });
    $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnReturnDay, #ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnReturnMonth").change(function() {
        setHiddenDate('ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnReturnDay', 'ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnReturnMonth', 'ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_hiddenReturnDate');
    });

    if (select2Enabled) {
        $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureCity").select2({formatResult: formatCountriesSelect2, matcher: select2CountryMatcher});
        $("#ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnArrivalCity").select2({formatResult: formatCountriesSelect2, matcher: select2CountryMatcher});
    }
    else {
        formatCountries("ctl00_MainContentRegion_MainRegion_epCenterColMiddleContentArea_ctl00_ctl02_ctl00_ipcAvaSearchBox_ddnDepartureCity");
    }
   
});

                    <h2><a href="/dk/rejseinformation/" class="page-header__link">N&#229;r du rejser med os</a></h2>
                <ul class="list  list--image-list  list--image-list--menu">
                    
    <li>
<i role="presentation" class="icon-medium icon-medium--baggage-checked-in"></i>            <h4>
                <a href="/dk/rejseinformation/bagage/" class="page-header__link  page-header__link--small">Bagage</a>
            </h4>

<p><span style="background-color: #d81939;"><span style="color: #ffffff; font-family: ApercuProRegular, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Hvor megen bagage, du kan have med, beskyttelse af din bagage til rejsen, og hvad du ikke skal pakke.</span></span></p>    </li>
    <li>
<i role="presentation" class="icon-medium icon-medium--fast-track"></i>            <h4>
                <a href="/dk/rejseinformation/indcheckning-og-boarding/" class="page-header__link  page-header__link--small">Indcheckning og boarding</a>
            </h4>

<p><span style="background-color: #d81939;"><span style="color: #ffffff; font-family: ApercuProRegular, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Hvornår, hvor og hvordan du checker ind, uanset om du er på nettet, i lufthavnen eller går direkte til din gate.</span></span></p>    </li>
    <li>
<i role="presentation" class="icon-medium icon-medium--special-needs"></i>            <h4>
                <a href="/dk/rejseinformation/specielle-behov/" class="page-header__link  page-header__link--small">S&#230;rlige behov</a>
            </h4>

<p><span style="background-color: #d81939;"><span style="color: #ffffff; font-family: ApercuProRegular, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Find ud af, hvordan du beder om assistance, hvis du har nedsat førlighed eller et handicap.</span></span></p>    </li>

                    
    <li>
        <h5>
            <a href="/dk/rejseinformation/" class="page-header__link  page-header__link--small">Se alle rejseoplysninger</a>
        </h5>
    </li>



                </ul>
            </section>
        </div>
    </nav>

                <ul class="list  list--image-list  list--image-list--menu">
                    
    <li>
<i role="presentation" class="icon-medium icon-medium--baggage-checked-in"></i>            <h3>
                <a href="/dk/rejseinformation/bagage/" class="page-header__link  page-header__link--small">Bagage</a>
            </h3>

<p><span style="background-color: #d81939;"><span style="color: #ffffff; font-family: ApercuProRegular, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Hvor megen bagage, du kan have med, beskyttelse af din bagage til rejsen, og hvad du ikke skal pakke.</span></span></p>    </li>
    <li>
<i role="presentation" class="icon-medium icon-medium--fast-track"></i>            <h3>
                <a href="/dk/rejseinformation/indcheckning-og-boarding/" class="page-header__link  page-header__link--small">Indcheckning og boarding</a>
            </h3>

<p><span style="background-color: #d81939;"><span style="color: #ffffff; font-family: ApercuProRegular, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Hvornår, hvor og hvordan du checker ind, uanset om du er på nettet, i lufthavnen eller går direkte til din gate.</span></span></p>    </li>
    <li>
<i role="presentation" class="icon-medium icon-medium--special-needs"></i>            <h3>
                <a href="/dk/rejseinformation/specielle-behov/" class="page-header__link  page-header__link--small">S&#230;rlige behov</a>
            </h3>

<p><span style="background-color: #d81939;"><span style="color: #ffffff; font-family: ApercuProRegular, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Find ud af, hvordan du beder om assistance, hvis du har nedsat førlighed eller et handicap.</span></span></p>    </li>

                    
    <li>
        <h3>
            <a href="/dk/rejseinformation/" class="page-header__link  page-header__link--small">Se alle rejseoplysninger</a>
        </h3>
    </li>



                </ul>
            </section>
        </div>
    </nav>
</header>
